<script nonce="">
  window.plausible = window.plausible || function() { (window.plausible.q = window.plausible.q || []).push(arguments); }
  const keyboardWhiteList = ['a', 'span', 'button']

  function getTaggedEventAttributes (e) {
    const eventAttrs = { name: null, props: {} }
    if (!e || !e.classList) return eventAttrs
    const psEvent = /plausible-event-(.+)(=|--)(.+)/
    for (const className of [...e.classList]) {
      const [, key, , val] = className.match(psEvent) || []
      if (!key || !val) continue
      const value = val.replace(/\+/g, ' ')
      switch (key.toLowerCase()) {
        case 'name':
          eventAttrs.name = value
          break
        default:
          eventAttrs.props[key] = value
          break
      }
    }
    return eventAttrs
  }

  function isLocal () {
    return /^localhost$|^127(\.[0-9]+){0,2}\.[0-9]+$|^\[::1?\]$/.test(location.hostname) || location.protocol === 'file:'
  }

  function isAutomation () {
    return Boolean(window._phantom || window.__nightmare || window.navigator.webdriver || window.Cypress)
  }

  function shouldIgnore () {
    return isLocal() ||
      isAutomation() ||
      window.localStorage.getItem('plausible_ignore') === 'true'
  }

  function handler (e) {
    if (!window.plausible) return
    if (!e.target || !('className' in e.target)) return
    const ele = e.target

    const eventAttrs = getTaggedEventAttributes(ele)
    if (!eventAttrs.name) return
    if (ele?.href) eventAttrs.props.url = ele.href

    if (shouldIgnore()) {
      if (window.debug) {
        console.warn(
          `Ignoring Event: "${eventAttrs.name}"`,
          { props: eventAttrs.props },
        )
      }
      return
    }
    window.plausible(eventAttrs.name, { props: eventAttrs.props })
  }

  function keydownHandler (e) {
    if (e.key !== 'Enter') return
    if (e.target.nodeName.toLowerCase() === 'input') {
      switch (e.target.type.toLowerCase()) {
        case 'submit':
        case 'button':
        case 'reset':
        case 'checkbox':
        case 'radio':
        case 'file':
        case 'image':
        case 'color':
          break
        default:
          return
      }
    } else if (!keyboardWhiteList.includes(e.target.nodeName.toLowerCase())) {
      return
    }
    handler(e)
  }

  document.addEventListener('mousedown', handler)
  document.addEventListener('keydown', keydownHandler)
</script>

SimpleTracker</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">9</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">2. GuideMe</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 13px;"><div class="CodeMirror-foldgutter-open CodeMirror-guttermarker-subtle"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-header cm-header-1"># New App Ideas - Evaluate and Categorize</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">13</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 44px; width: 13px;"><div class="CodeMirror-foldgutter-open CodeMirror-guttermarker-subtle"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-header cm-header-3">### 1. SmartSpend </span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">14</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">- </span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-strong cm-variable-2">**Category:**</span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2"> Finance/Productivity App</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">15</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">- </span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-strong cm-variable-2">**Mobile:**</span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2"> View and edit features.</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">16</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">- </span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-strong cm-variable-2">**Story:**</span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2"> The app seeks to simplify the understanding of personal expenses, empowering users to take charge of their finances effortlessly. By offering intuitive features and clear insights, it aims to transform the daunting task of budgeting into a manageable and even enjoyable experience.</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">17</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">- </span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-strong cm-variable-2">**Market:**</span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2"> All individuals, especially students,who desire a straightforward solution for tracking expenses and managing budgets.</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">18</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">- </span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-strong cm-variable-2">**Habit:**</span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2"> The app encourages users to develop consistent habits of tracking expenses, setting realistic budgets, and making informed financial decisions.</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">19</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">- </span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-strong cm-variable-2">**Scope:**</span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2"> The app's scope encompasses essential features such as expense categorization, customizable budget creation, real-time spending updates, goal setting, and personalized financial recommendations. </span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">20</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="">​</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">21</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 44px; width: 13px;"><div class="CodeMirror-foldgutter-open CodeMirror-guttermarker-subtle"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-header cm-header-3">### 2. GuideMe</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">22</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">- </span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-strong cm-variable-2">**Category:**</span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2"> Travel/Discovery App</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">23</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">- </span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-strong cm-variable-2">**Mobile:**</span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2"> Explore and discover new destinations, view recommendations, and plan your trip on the go.</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">24</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">- </span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-strong cm-variable-2">**Story:**</span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2"> Aims to assist travelers in finding their next vacation destination by providing curated lists of top places to visit, along with recommendations for hotels, restaurants, and attractions.</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">25</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">- </span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-strong cm-variable-2">**Market:**</span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2"> Targeting travelers who are indecisive or unsure about where to go for their next vacation, Guide Me caters to a wide range of demographics, from solo adventurers to families and couples.</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">26</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">- </span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-strong cm-variable-2">**Habit:**</span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2"> Not usual, but encourages users to explore new destinations and plan their trips  by providing inspiration and practical recommendations. By using the app, users can also develop a habit of researching and discovering new places to visit.</span></span></pre></div><div style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-wrapper" aria-hidden="true" style="left: -58px;"><div class="CodeMirror-linenumber CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 0px; width: 28px;">27</div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-elt" style="left: 36px; width: 8px;"><div style="height: 100%;" class="authorship-gutter authorship-gutter-58f496" title="" data-original-title="AdityaRaj Padmanabhan"></div></div></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2">- </span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-strong cm-variable-2">**Scope:**</span><span class="cm-m-markdown cm-variable-2"> The app enables users to choose between international or domestic destinations, explore continents, and discover top places to visit. It provides information on hotels, restaurants, and attractions, with options to save favorite destinations and access user reviews for enhanced travel planning.</span></span></pre></div></div></div></div></div></div><div style="position: absolute; height: 50px; width: 1px; border-bottom: 0px solid transparent; top: 2129px;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutters" style="left: 0px; height: 2179px;"><div class="CodeMirror-gutter CodeMirror-linenumbers" style="width: 36px;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter authorship-gutters"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter CodeMirror-foldgutter"></div></div></div></div><div class="container-thin template-menu" style="display: none;">

        <div id="doc" class="markdown-body container-fluid comment-inner comment-enabled" data-hard-breaks="true"><h1 class="part in-view" data-startline="1" data-endline="1" id="Favorite-Applications-of-Interests" data-id="Favorite-Applications-of-Interests"><a class="anchor hidden-xs" href="https://hackmd.io/Uek2Nos4RLy2JRfOuINFGw?both#Favorite-Applications-of-Interests" title="Favorite-Applications-of-Interests" smoothhashscroll=""><span class="octicon octicon-link"></span></a><span data-position="2" data-size="34">Favorite Applications of Interests</span></h1><ol class="part in-view" data-startline="3" data-endline="6" data-position="38" data-size="0">
<li class="" data-startline="3" data-endline="3" data-position="41" data-size="0"><span data-position="41" data-size="6">Notion</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="4" data-endline="4" data-position="51" data-size="0"><span data-position="51" data-size="5">Notes</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="5" data-endline="6" data-position="61" data-size="0"><span data-position="61" data-size="9">Reminders</span></li>
</ol><h1 class="part in-view" data-startline="7" data-endline="7" id="New-App-Ideas" data-id="New-App-Ideas"><a class="anchor hidden-xs" href="https://hackmd.io/Uek2Nos4RLy2JRfOuINFGw?both#New-App-Ideas" title="New-App-Ideas" smoothhashscroll=""><span class="octicon octicon-link"></span></a><span data-position="74" data-size="13">New App Ideas</span></h1><ol class="part in-view" data-startline="8" data-endline="11" data-position="89" data-size="0">
<li class="" data-startline="8" data-endline="8" data-position="92" data-size="0"><span data-position="92" data-size="13">SimpleTracker</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="9" data-endline="9" data-position="109" data-size="0"><span data-position="109" data-size="8">EasyNote</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="10" data-endline="11" data-position="121" data-size="0"><span data-position="121" data-size="7">GuideMe</span></li>
</ol><h1 class="part in-view" data-startline="12" data-endline="12" id="New-App-Ideas---Evaluate-and-Categorize" data-id="New-App-Ideas---Evaluate-and-Categorize"><a class="anchor hidden-xs" href="https://hackmd.io/Uek2Nos4RLy2JRfOuINFGw?both#New-App-Ideas---Evaluate-and-Categorize" title="New-App-Ideas---Evaluate-and-Categorize" smoothhashscroll=""><span class="octicon octicon-link"></span></a><span data-position="132" data-size="39">New App Ideas - Evaluate and Categorize</span></h1><h3 class="part in-view" data-startline="13" data-endline="13" id="1-SmartSpend" data-id="1-SmartSpend"><a class="anchor hidden-xs" href="https://hackmd.io/Uek2Nos4RLy2JRfOuINFGw?both#1-SmartSpend" title="1-SmartSpend" smoothhashscroll=""><span class="octicon octicon-link"></span></a><span data-position="176" data-size="13">1. SmartSpend</span></h3><ul class="part in-view" data-startline="14" data-endline="20" data-position="191" data-size="0">
<li class="" data-startline="14" data-endline="14" data-position="193" data-size="0"><strong data-position="193" data-size="0"><span data-position="195" data-size="9">Category:</span></strong><span data-position="206" data-size="25"> Finance/Productivity App</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="15" data-endline="15" data-position="234" data-size="0"><strong data-position="234" data-size="0"><span data-position="236" data-size="7">Mobile:</span></strong><span data-position="245" data-size="24"> View and edit features.</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="16" data-endline="16" data-position="272" data-size="0"><strong data-position="272" data-size="0"><span data-position="274" data-size="6">Story:</span></strong><span data-position="282" data-size="282"> The app seeks to simplify the understanding of personal expenses, empowering users to take charge of their finances effortlessly. By offering intuitive features and clear insights, it aims to transform the daunting task of budgeting into a manageable and even enjoyable experience.</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="17" data-endline="17" data-position="567" data-size="0"><strong data-position="567" data-size="0"><span data-position="569" data-size="7">Market:</span></strong><span data-position="578" data-size="119"> All individuals, especially students,who desire a straightforward solution for tracking expenses and managing budgets.</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="18" data-endline="18" data-position="700" data-size="0"><strong data-position="700" data-size="0"><span data-position="702" data-size="6">Habit:</span></strong><span data-position="710" data-size="144"> The app encourages users to develop consistent habits of tracking expenses, setting realistic budgets, and making informed financial decisions.</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="19" data-endline="20" data-position="857" data-size="0"><strong data-position="857" data-size="0"><span data-position="859" data-size="6">Scope:</span></strong><span data-position="867" data-size="195"> The app's scope encompasses essential features such as expense categorization, customizable budget creation, real-time spending updates, goal setting, and personalized financial recommendations.</span></li>
</ul><h3 class="part in-view" data-startline="21" data-endline="21" id="2-GuideMe" data-id="2-GuideMe"><a class="anchor hidden-xs" href="https://hackmd.io/Uek2Nos4RLy2JRfOuINFGw?both#2-GuideMe" title="2-GuideMe" smoothhashscroll=""><span class="octicon octicon-link"></span></a><span data-position="1069" data-size="10">2. GuideMe</span></h3><ul class="part in-view" data-startline="22" data-endline="27" data-position="1080" data-size="0">
<li class="" data-startline="22" data-endline="22" data-position="1082" data-size="0"><strong data-position="1082" data-size="0"><span data-position="1084" data-size="9">Category:</span></strong><span data-position="1095" data-size="21"> Travel/Discovery App</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="23" data-endline="23" data-position="1119" data-size="0"><strong data-position="1119" data-size="0"><span data-position="1121" data-size="7">Mobile:</span></strong><span data-position="1130" data-size="91"> Explore and discover new destinations, view recommendations, and plan your trip on the go.</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="24" data-endline="24" data-position="1224" data-size="0"><strong data-position="1224" data-size="0"><span data-position="1226" data-size="6">Story:</span></strong><span data-position="1234" data-size="188"> Aims to assist travelers in finding their next vacation destination by providing curated lists of top places to visit, along with recommendations for hotels, restaurants, and attractions.</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="25" data-endline="25" data-position="1425" data-size="0"><strong data-position="1425" data-size="0"><span data-position="1427" data-size="7">Market:</span></strong><span data-position="1436" data-size="188"> Targeting travelers who are indecisive or unsure about where to go for their next vacation, Guide Me caters to a wide range of demographics, from solo adventurers to families and couples.</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="26" data-endline="26" data-position="1627" data-size="0"><strong data-position="1627" data-size="0"><span data-position="1629" data-size="6">Habit:</span></strong><span data-position="1637" data-size="239"> Not usual, but encourages users to explore new destinations and plan their trips  by providing inspiration and practical recommendations. By using the app, users can also develop a habit of researching and discovering new places to visit.</span></li>
<li class="" data-startline="27" data-endline="27" data-position="1879" data-size="0"><strong data-position="1879" data-size="0"><span data-position="1881" data-size="6">Scope:</span></strong><span data-position="1889" data-size="296"> The app enables users to choose between international or domestic destinations, explore continents, and discover top places to visit. It provides information on hotels, restaurants, and attractions, with options to save favorite destinations and access user reviews for enhanced travel planning.</span></li>
</ul></div>

<script id="gsi-client" src="./Activity1_files/client" async="" defer="" nonce=""></script>
<script nonce="">
    function handleCredentialResponse(response) {
        const form = document.getElementById('sign-in-with-google-form')
        form.children.credential.value = response.credential
        form.children.method.value = location.href.toLowerCase() === 'https://hackmd.io/settings#general' ? 'merge' : 'login'
        form.submit()
    }
    var GSI_READY = new Promise(function (resolve) {
        function initialize () {
            google.accounts.id.initialize({
                client_id: '911617723593-drikdibvvn63slfd6kbqigo8ql1no55s.apps.googleusercontent.com',
                callback: handleCredentialResponse
            })
            const loginPath = 'https://hackmd.io/login'
            const joinPath = 'https://hackmd.io/join'
            const renderButton = function () {
                google.accounts.id.renderButton(
                    document.getElementById('sign-in-with-google-button'),
                    { type: 'standard', width: 250 }
                )
            }
            if (location.href.toLowerCase() === loginPath || location.href.toLowerCase() === joinPath) {
                renderButton()
            } else {
                $('.signin-modal').one('shown.bs.modal', function () {
                    renderButton()
                })
            }
            resolve()
        }

        window.addEventListener('load', function () { initialize() })
    })
</script>
<form class="hidden" id="sign-in-with-google-form" action="https://hackmd.io/auth/google" method="post">
    <input type="hidden" name="credential">
    <input type="hidden" name="method">
</form>

<script nonce="">
  (function () {
    function onSubmit (e) {
      const submitButton = e.target
      const tokenInput = document.getElementById('recaptcha-token')
      if (tokenInput.value) return

      e.preventDefault()
      grecaptcha.enterprise.ready(async () => {
        const token = await grecaptcha.enterprise.execute('6LdtkK4ZAAAAAG1B4iENhmQTce1xNTyHu0GjgnXi', {action: 'login'})
        tokenInput.value = token
        submitButton.click()
      })
    }
    document.querySelectorAll('#signin-form input[type="submit"]').forEach((el) => {
      el.addEventListener('click', onSubmit)
    })
  })()
</script>


        </div>
    </div>

                                </tr>

                                    <td class="example-syntax">1. Ordered List</td>

                                </tr>

                                    <td class="example-syntax">- [ ] Todo List</td>

                                    <td class="hidden-xs"></td>
                                </tr>

                                    <td class="example-syntax">&gt; Blockquote</td>
                                    <td class="example-present"><blockquote style="margin: 0;"> Blockquote</blockquote></td>
                                    <td class="hidden-xs"></td>
                                </tr>
                                <tr>
                                    <td class="example-syntax">**Bold font**</td>

                                    <td class="hidden-xs"></td>
                                </tr>

                                    <td class="example-syntax">*Italics font*</td>

                                    <td class="hidden-xs"></td>
                                </tr>

                                    <td class="example-syntax">~~Strikethrough~~</td>
                                    <td class="example-present"><s>Strikethrough</s></td>
                                    <td class="hidden-xs"></td>
                                </tr>
                                <tr>
                                    <td class="example-syntax">19^th^</td>
                                    <td class="example-present">19<sup>th</sup></td>
                                    <td class="hidden-xs"></td>
                                </tr>

                                    <td class="example-syntax">H~2~O</td>
                                    <td class="example-present">H<sub>2</sub>O</td>
                                    <td class="hidden-xs"></td>
                                </tr>

                                    <td class="example-syntax">++Inserted text++</td>

                                    <td class="hidden-xs"></td>
                                </tr>

                                    <td class="hidden-xs"></td>

                                    <td class="hidden-xs"></td>
                                </tr>

                                    <td class="example-present">Image</td>
                                    <td class="hidden-xs"></td>
                                </tr>

                                    <td class="example-syntax">`Code`</td>
                                    <td class="example-present"><code>Code</code></td>

                                </tr>
                                <tr>
                                    <td class="example-syntax">```javascript<br>var i = 0;<br>```</td>

                                    <td class="hidden-xs"></td>
